<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Attached are NVIDIA Corporation&#146;s materials related to a proposed tender offer (the &#147;Preliminary
Communications&#148;) pursuant to which NVIDIA would offer to amend, at the election of the applicable option holder, certain portions of options to purchase NVIDIA common stock granted under the NVIDIA Corporation 1998 Equity Incentive Plan, as
amended (the &#147;Plan&#148;) that (a)&nbsp;were granted to former MediaQ employees at a discount in 2003, (b)&nbsp;vest or vested after December&nbsp;31, 2004, and (c)&nbsp;are still outstanding on the date the proposed tender offer expires (the
&#147;Eligible Options&#148;). Option holders who elect to amend their options will sign an amendment to their existing option agreement with NVIDIA, pursuant to which portions of such options will be amended to expire within 2<FONT
SIZE="1"><SUP>&nbsp;1</SUP></FONT><FONT SIZE="2">/</FONT><FONT SIZE="1">2</FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2" COLOR="#000000"> months after the close of the calendar year in which the portions vest. </FONT></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The Preliminary Communications do not constitute an offer to holders of options to purchase
NVIDIA common stock to amend their options. In the event the NVIDIA Board of Directors approves the tender offer, the tender offer may be commenced at such time as determined in the discretion of the NVIDIA Board of Directors. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>At the time the tender offer has commenced, NVIDIA will provide option holders who are
eligible to participate in the tender offer with written materials explaining the precise terms and timing of the tender offer. Persons who are eligible to participate in the tender offer should read these written materials carefully when they
become available because they will contain important information about the tender offer.&nbsp;NVIDIA will also file these written materials with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission as part of a tender offer statement upon the commencement of
the tender offer. NVIDIA stockholders and option holders will be able to obtain these written materials and other documents filed by NVIDIA with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission free of charge from the U.S. Securities and Exchange
Commission&#146;s website at www.sec.gov.&nbsp;In addition, stockholders and option holders may request a free copy of the tender offer statement and other documents related to the tender offer from NVIDIA following such time that such documents
become available. </B></FONT></P>

<DESCRIPTION>MEMORANDUM FROM JENSEN HUANG TO EMPLOYEES
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Memorandum from Jensen Huang to Employees</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EXHIBIT 99.1 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" ALIGN="center">

<TR>
<TD WIDTH="6%"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="2%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="92%"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>To:</B></FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Employee Name (EE#)</FONT></P></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>From:</B></FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Jensen Huang</FONT></P></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD HEIGHT="16"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="16" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR>
<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Subject:</B></FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE="margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Section 409A &#150; Discounted Stock Options</FONT></P></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">You are receiving this notice because
you were granted discounted stock options as a result of the acquisition of MediaQ by NVIDIA in 2003. As a result of recent changes to the Internal Revenue Code (the &#147;Code&#148;), the stock option grant you received at the time of the
acquisition is now considered to be out of compliance with Section&nbsp;409A of the Code (&#147;Section 409A&#148;) and, as a result, may be subject to punitive tax treatment under Section&nbsp;409A. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Section&nbsp;409A was added to the Code by the American Jobs Creation Act of 2004. In
September 2005, the U.S. Treasury Department and Internal Revenue Service issued proposed regulations under Section&nbsp;409A. The proposed regulations covering Section&nbsp;409A provide that stock options that vest after December&nbsp;31, 2004 that
were issued with an exercise price that is less than the related fair market value on the date of grant (meaning they were issued at a discount) generally are deferred compensation that is not in compliance with Section&nbsp;409A and will likely
result in income recognition by you prior to exercise, an additional twenty percent (20%) tax, and potential interest charges. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Section&nbsp;409A specifically applies to discounted stock options granted prior to October&nbsp;4, 2004, if vesting occurs on or after January&nbsp;1, 2005. However,
only the portions of the discounted option grant that vest in or after 2005 are subject to Section&nbsp;409A. The portion of a discounted option grant made prior to October&nbsp;4, 2004 and that vested prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005 is grandfathered
and, as a result, is exempt from Section&nbsp;409A. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Because a portion of the
discounted option grant you received vests in, or after, 2005, NVIDIA is offering to amend your stock option grant. <B>If you do not accept the offer, you may face immediate income taxation on the full spread between your exercise price and the fair
market value of our common stock at the time of vesting, </B><B><I>regardless of whether you exercise the stock option at vesting</I></B><B>, as well as a 20% additional tax and a potential interest penalty on the same amount of income</B>. These
taxes and penalties may continue to accrue for each year that you continue to have unexercised, discounted stock options. Because of these potential taxes and penalties, NVIDIA intends to offer to amend your stock option such that it will be
compliant with Section&nbsp;409A. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Included in the materials that follow are: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<DESCRIPTION>NVIDIA RESPONSE TO SECTION 409A COMPLIANCE
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>NVIDIA Response to Section 409A Compliance</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EXHIBIT 99.2 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>NVIDIA Response to Section&nbsp;409A Compliance </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Vested Grandfathered Discounted Stock Options </U></B><U>(Options vesting prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005)<B> </B></U></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Discounted stock options vested prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005 are considered grandfathered
under Section&nbsp;409A and, therefore, are exempt from taxation or penalty under that provision. Therefore, all discounted stock options granted by NVIDIA that vested prior to January&nbsp;1, 2005 will continue to exist with the six year term
identified in your original grant agreement. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Vested Non-Grandfathered
Discounted Stock Options </U></B><U>(Options vesting between 1/1/05 and 12/31/05)<B> </B></U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Discounted stock options that vested in 2005 are potentially subject to the tax consequences of Section&nbsp;409A. To avoid such penalties you will have two alternatives to consider: </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">1.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Exercise all discounted stock options that vested in 2005 prior to December&nbsp;31, 2005 </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Consent to amend the expiration date on discounted stock options that vested in 2005 to March&nbsp;15, 2006 (See note below) </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If you choose not to accept one of these alternatives, <B>you may face immediate income
taxation on the full spread between your exercise price and the fair market value of our common stock at the time of vesting, </B><B><I>regardless of whether you exercise the stock option at vesting</I></B><B>, as well as a 20% additional tax and a
potential interest penalty on the same amount of income</B>. If applicable, these taxes and penalties will continue to accrue for each year that you continue to hold vested unexercised discounted stock options. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%; text-indent:-2%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><U><B>Unvested Non-Grandfathered Discounted Stock Options
</B>(Options vesting January&nbsp;1, 2006 and later) </U></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">NVIDIA is offering
to amend your unvested discounted stock options by amending the 6-year term identified in your original grant agreement as follows: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">1.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Shares Vesting in Calendar Year 2006</B> - New Expiration Date: March&nbsp;15, 2007 </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Shares Vesting in Calendar Year 2007</B> - New Expiration Date: March&nbsp;15, 2008 </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">3.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Shares Vesting in Calendar Year 2008</B> - New Expiration Date: March&nbsp;15, 2009 </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Amending your discounted stock option agreement such that it will expire within 2-1/2 months after the close of the calendar year in which
it vests will reduce the time in which you have to exercise the options, (transactions must be completed prior to and not including the new expiration dates), but may eliminate your exposure to Section&nbsp;409A liability by bringing your discounted
stock option grant into compliance with a short-term deferral provision under Section&nbsp;409A. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Note:</B> Because this approach changes the terms of your original agreement NVIDIA intends to conduct a tender offer in January 2006 to obtain your consent for the amendment to your discounted stock option grant.
Additional information regarding the tender offer and your rights and responsibilities will be forthcoming in January. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>NVIDIA Response to Section&nbsp;409A Compliance (continued) </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Supplemental Option Grant </U></B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Amending the expiration date of your discounted stock options to be 409A-compliant may
affect the return you might have realized had compliance not been required. Although the need for such an amendment was created by the enactment of Section&nbsp;409A and not by any action taken by NVIDIA, NVIDIA has decided to offer you a
Supplemental Option Grant in acknowledgement of the reduced term. Details of your Supplemental Grant are outlined in the document on the page that follows. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>At the time the tender offer has commenced, NVIDIA will provide option holders who are eligible to participate in the tender offer with written materials explaining
the precise terms and timing of the tender offer. Persons who are eligible to participate in the tender offer should read these written materials carefully when they become available because they will contain important information about the tender
offer.&nbsp;NVIDIA will also file these written materials with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission as part of a tender offer statement upon the commencement of the tender offer. NVIDIA stockholders and option holders will be able to obtain
these written materials and other documents filed by NVIDIA with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission free of charge from the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission&#146;s website at www.sec.gov.&nbsp;In addition, stockholders and option
holders may request a free copy of the tender offer statement and other documents related to the tender offer from NVIDIA following such time that such documents become available. </I></FONT></P>

will be viewable to you at www.benefitaccess.com within 10 - 15 business days of your receipt of this memo. This website is administered by Smith Barney Stock Plan Services, our external stock plan administrator. </FONT></P> <P

Section&nbsp;409A, or the possible amendment of your discounted stock option, please contact Suzie Bentley at (408)&nbsp;566-6591 or Melissa Riley at (408)&nbsp;486-2791. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:2%; text-indent:-2%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Thank you. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P

<DOCUMENT>
<TYPE>EX-99.6
<SEQUENCE>7
<FILENAME>dex996.htm
<DESCRIPTION>FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS: SECTION 409A
<TEXT>
<HTML><HEAD>
<TITLE>Frequently Asked Questions: Section 409A</TITLE>
</HEAD>
 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="right"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">EXHIBIT 99.6 </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Frequently Asked Questions: Section&nbsp;409A </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Why do I need to be concerned about Section&nbsp;409A compliance? </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Section&nbsp;409A of the Internal Revenue Code (&#147;Section 409A&#148;), which was enacted in October 2004, contains a provision regarding discounted stock option
grants. As part of NVIDIA&#146;s acquisition of MediaQ you were awarded a discounted stock option that, because of Section&nbsp;409A, will have adverse tax consequences for you if it does not now become compliant with Section&nbsp;409A. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>What is Section&nbsp;409A and what are the effects on our discounted options?
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In October 2004, the American Jobs Creation Act (&#147;Act&#148;) went
into effect. The Act contained language that has become part of the Internal Revenue Code (&#147;IRC&#148;) at Section&nbsp;409A and significantly changed the tax rules applicable to unfunded, nonqualified deferred compensation arrangements. Most
significant to NVIDIA, Section&nbsp;409A and the regulations related to Section&nbsp;409A that were proposed by the Internal Revenue Service dramatically expanded the definition of deferred compensation to include stock options that were granted at
a discount from the fair market value at the time of grant. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Section&nbsp;409A
applies to all discounted stock options granted prior to October&nbsp;4, 2004, if they vest on or after January&nbsp;1, 2005. In our case, NVIDIA acquired MediaQ and granted stock options to former MediaQ employees at a discount in 2003. These
grants vest quarterly in 2003, 2004, 2005, 2006, and 2007. Only the portions of the discounted stock option grant that vest in 2005 and later are subject to Section&nbsp;409A. The portion of the stock option grant that vested in 2003 and 2004 is
exempt from Section&nbsp;409A. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Because a portion of the discounted option
grant you received vests in, or after, 2005, NVIDIA is offering to amend your stock option grant. <B>If you do not accept the offer, you may face immediate income taxation on the full spread between your exercise price and the fair market value of
our common stock at the time of vesting, </B><B><I>regardless of whether you exercise the stock option at vesting</I></B><B>, as well as a 20% additional tax and a potential interest penalty on the same amount of income</B>. These taxes and
penalties may continue to accrue for each year that you continue to have unexercised, discounted stock options. Because of these potential taxes and penalties, NVIDIA is offering to amend your stock option such that it will be compliant with
Section&nbsp;409A. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>What is NVIDIA doing to make our discounted options
Section&nbsp;409A compliant? </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">NVIDIA intends to offer to amend the 6-year
term identified in your original grant agreement as follows: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">1.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Shares Vesting in Calendar Year 2005</B> - New Expiration Date: March&nbsp;15, 2006 </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Shares Vesting in Calendar Year 2006</B> - New Expiration Date: March&nbsp;15, 2007 </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">3.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Shares Vesting in Calendar Year 2007</B> - New Expiration Date: March&nbsp;15, 2008 </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">4.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Shares Vesting in Calendar Year 2008</B> - New Expiration Date: March&nbsp;15, 2009 </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Frequently Asked Questions: Section&nbsp;409A (continued) </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Amending your discounted stock option agreement such that it will expire within 2-1/2 months
after the close of the calendar year in which it vests will reduce the time in which you have to exercise the options, (transactions must be completed prior to and not including the new expiration dates), but may eliminate your exposure to
Section&nbsp;409A liability by bringing your discounted stock option grant into compliance with a short-term deferral provision under Section&nbsp;409A. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Note:</B> Because this approach changes the terms of your original agreement NVIDIA intends to conduct a tender offer in January 2006 to obtain your consent for the
amendment to your discounted stock option grant. Additional information regarding the proposed tender offer and your rights and responsibilities will be forthcoming in January. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Is there anything else I can do with my options that vested in 2005 to avoid the potential tax penalties of Section&nbsp;409A?
</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Discounted stock options that vested in 2005 are potentially subject to
the tax consequences of Section&nbsp;409A. To avoid such penalties you will have two alternatives to consider: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">1.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Exercise all discounted stock options that vested in 2005 prior to December&nbsp;31, 2005. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">2.</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Consent to amend the expiration date on discounted stock options that vested in 2005 to March&nbsp;15, 2006 (See note below). </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">If you choose not to accept one of these alternatives, <B>you may face immediate income
taxation on the full spread between your exercise price and the fair market value of our common stock at the time of vesting, </B><B><I>regardless of whether you exercise the stock option at vesting</I></B><B>, as well as a 20% additional tax and a
potential interest penalty on the same amount of income</B>. If applicable, these taxes and penalties will continue to accrue for each year that you continue to hold vested unexercised discounted stock options. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Note:</B> Because this approach changes the terms of your original agreement NVIDIA
intends to conduct a tender offer in January 2006 to obtain your consent for the amendment to your discounted stock option grant. Additional information regarding the proposed tender offer and your rights and responsibilities will be forthcoming in
January. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Where can I find out if I have exercised my discounted options
that vested in 2005? </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Details of your discounted stock option grant can be
viewed online at www.benefitaccess.com. From your account you can view both the vesting and exercise activity related to your discounted stock option award. If by December&nbsp;31, 2005, you exercise at least the same number of discounted stock
options that vest between January&nbsp;1, 2005 and December&nbsp;31, 2005&#151;or if, pursuant to the proposed tender offer, you agree to modify that same number of discounted stock options to have an expiration date of March&nbsp;15, 2006, whether
or not you choose to exercise such options&#151;you should have protected those discounted stock options from taxes and penalties under Section&nbsp;409A. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Frequently Asked Questions: Section&nbsp;409A (continued) </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>What happens if my vesting schedule changes due to a Leave of Absence or a permanent
reduction in Standard Work Hours? </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">An interruption to the vesting schedule
of your discounted stock option may cause a portion of your options to vest in a later calendar year than originally calculated. As a result, should you consent to bring such options into compliance with the short-term deferral provision through the
proposed tender offer process, the expiration date related to those options would also be delayed so that, generally speaking, the options would expire 2<FONT SIZE="1"><SUP>&nbsp;1</SUP></FONT><FONT SIZE="2">/</FONT><FONT SIZE="1">2</FONT><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2" COLOR="#000000"> months following the end of the calendar year in which they actually vest. </FONT></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>What are my exercise alternatives? </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">You have several alternatives when considering the exercise of your stock option. Below are some common considerations. For a complete listing as well as additional
details of each method please access www.benefitaccess.com. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Cash
Exercise:</U></B> Allows you to use your personal savings or other funds to exercise any of your exercisable stock options. The exercise occurs upon your request; however, cleared funds must be in your brokerage account to conduct this type of
transaction. The shares purchased will be deposited into your brokerage account. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exercise and Hold:</B> An Exercise and Hold is a cash exercise method that allows you to exercise your stock options and hold the resulting shares. This type of transaction requires payment of the option cost and
applicable withholding taxes prior to exercise but will result in you owning a number of shares of common stock equal to the number of shares you elected to exercise. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><U>Cashless Exercise: </U></B>Allows you to receive the value of your stock options or obtain shares of Company stock without any cash
outlay. With a cashless exercise, you purchase shares of Company stock at the grant price and simultaneously sell them at the market price. You can either receive cash or use the proceeds to purchase additional shares of Company stock. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Exercise and Sell to Cover:</B> A cashless exercise method that allows
you to exercise a quantity of options and sell just enough of the resulting shares to cover the cost of the option as well as any applicable taxes. This type of transaction will result in you owning a reduced number of common shares from your
original option amount because you will have used a portion of your shares to pay the costs of acquiring the shares you are holding. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Frequently Asked Questions: Section&nbsp;409A (continued) </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Who should I contact if I have additional questions? </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">A representative from the Deloitte Tax Group will be conducting a one hour informational
session at the Santa Clara Campus on Wednesday, December&nbsp;14th. This will be your best opportunity to get clarification on the ramifications of Section&nbsp;409A and our response. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Additional questions regarding our plan for reducing your 409A exposure should be directed to the HR-Consultant for your business group.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">For information regarding your vesting and/or exercise activity, please
contact Anca Bacila in Stock Administration. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Finally, you are encouraged to
consult your personal Financial/Tax Advisor for guidance specific to your situation. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2"><I>At the time the tender offer has commenced, NVIDIA will provide option holders who are eligible to participate in the tender offer with written materials explaining the precise terms and timing of the tender offer. Persons who are
eligible to participate in the tender offer should read these written materials carefully when they become available because they will contain important information about the tender offer.&nbsp;NVIDIA will also file these written materials with the
U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission as part of a tender offer statement upon the commencement of the tender offer. NVIDIA stockholders and option holders will be able to obtain these written materials and other documents filed by NVIDIA with the
U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission free of charge from the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission&#146;s website at www.sec.gov.&nbsp;In addition, stockholders and option holders may request a free copy of the tender offer statement and other
documents related to the tender offer from NVIDIA following such time that such documents become available. </I></FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>Hypothetical Example: Tax Penalties and Withholdings of 409A Non-Compliance </B></FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Based on the scenario above employees who do not exercise their discounted stock options in
accordance with Section&nbsp;409A would potentially double the total taxes owed for their exercise and sale. Additionally, it is important to note that both the estimated income tax and the additional tax are considered <B>due at vesting</B>, which
could require a cash payment from the option holder prior to any gain actually being realized. Although the Estimated Income Tax prepayment is in theory &#147;trued up&#148; at the time of sale, which could result in a refund of any overpayment, no
such provision exists for the additional tax. As a result, should the FMV at exercise be lower than the FMV at the time of vesting or should the option vest and expire unexercised, the additional tax remains payable in the amounts calculated when
the options vested and would not be reduced or refunded to the employee. Finally, should an employee opt to not pay the estimated income and additional taxes at the time the stock options vest it is possible that additional IRS mandated interest and
penalties may be assessed. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B><I>The information set forth in
this example is hypothetical and is intended only to illustrate the potential impact of Section&nbsp;409A non-compliance. Since final guidance regarding the timing of 409A related taxes has not been issued, the actual impact could vary significantly
from what is indicated. </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><I>At the time the tender offer has commenced,
NVIDIA will provide option holders who are eligible to participate in the tender offer with written materials explaining the precise terms and timing of the tender offer. Persons who are eligible to participate in the tender offer should read these
written materials carefully when they become available because they will contain important information about the tender offer.&nbsp;NVIDIA will also file these written materials with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission as part of a tender
offer statement upon the commencement of the tender offer. NVIDIA stockholders and option holders will be able to obtain these written materials and other documents filed by NVIDIA with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission free of charge from
the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission&#146;s website at www.sec.gov.&nbsp;In addition, stockholders and option holders may request a free copy of the tender offer statement and other documents related to the tender offer from NVIDIA following
such time that such documents become available. </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2" COLOR="#000000">FMV = Estimated market value at vesting date. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

style='position:absolute;left:117px;top:238px;font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-size:27px;font-family:arial,"times new roman",times,serif;color:#FFFFFF;'>Only the portions of the discounted option grant that vest in or</div> <div
style='position:absolute;left:117px;top:267px;font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-size:27px;font-family:arial,"times new roman",times,serif;color:#FFFFFF;'>after 2005 are subject to Section 409A.&nbsp; </div> <div
style='position:absolute;left:117px;top:302px;font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-size:27px;font-family:arial,"times new roman",times,serif;color:#FFFFFF;'>The portion of a discounted option grant made prior to 10/4/04 </div> <div
style='position:absolute;left:117px;top:331px;font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-size:27px;font-family:arial,"times new roman",times,serif;color:#FFFFFF;'>and that vested prior to 1/1/05 are considered grandfathered </div> <div
style='position:absolute;left:117px;top:359px;font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-size:27px;font-family:arial,"times new roman",times,serif;color:#FFFFFF;'>under Section 409A and, therefore, are exempt from taxation </div> <div
style='position:absolute;left:117px;top:388px;font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-size:27px;font-family:arial,"times new roman",times,serif;color:#FFFFFF;'>or penalty under that provision.</div> <div
style='position:absolute;left:117px;top:459px;font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-size:27px;font-family:arial,"times new roman",times,serif;color:#FFFFFF;'>As a result portions of your discounted option grant can be </div> <div
style='position:absolute;left:117px;top:487px;font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-size:27px;font-family:arial,"times new roman",times,serif;color:#FFFFFF;'>grouped into the three categories below:</div> <div
style='position:absolute;left:171px;top:522px;font-style:normal;font-weight:bold;font-size:24px;font-family:arial,"times new roman",times,serif;color:#FFFFFF;'>Vested Grandfathered: Discounted options vested prior to </div> <div
